2.4.4 Formål med lenke (3 avvik)
Testregel 2.4.4 (2.4.4 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Link opens in new window without indication

<a class="tv2-menu__pill tv2-menu__context-link tv2-menu__context-link--tv2play" href="https://play.tv2.no/" id="tv2-menu-play-link" target="_blank">TV 2 Play</a>
Add text like '(opens in new tab)' or use visually-hidden text for screen readers
Testregel 2.4.4 (2.4.4 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

Link text is not descriptive: 'Info'

<a class="tv2-menu__megamenu__link" href="https://info.tv2.no"><span>Info</span></a>
Use descriptive text that indicates where the link goes (e.g., 'Read more about products' instead of 'Read more')
Testregel 2.4.4 (2.4.4 - Nivå A)
MINOR

Link text has redundant phrase: 'Gå tiltv2.no/semer'

<a class="webtease__link" href="https://www.tv2.no/semer/"><span class="webtease__link-text">Gå til </span>tv2.no/semer</a>
Remove 'link to' or similar - screen readers already announce it as a link

MODERATE

Heading level skipped: h1 to h3

<h3 class="svelte-snimg7">Kamper</h3>
Don't skip heading levels. Use h2 instead of h3
